theory spthy begin

// Function signature and definition of the equational theory E

functions: fst/1, pair/2, sdec/2, senc/2, snd/1
equations:
    fst(<x.1, x.2>) = x.1,
    sdec(senc(x.1, x.2), x.2) = x.1,
    snd(<x.1, x.2>) = x.2



rule (modulo E) init:
   [ Fr( ~runid ), Fr( ~Kab ), Fr( ~secret ) ]
  --[ Principals( ~runid, $Bob, $Alice ) ]->
   [
   !Bob_init( ~runid, $Bob, ~Kab ), !PrincipalPrivate( $Bob, ~Kab ),
   !Alice_init( ~runid, $Alice, ~Kab, ~secret ),
   !PrincipalPrivate( $Alice, ~Kab ), !PrincipalPrivate( $Alice, ~secret )
   ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Bob_2_0:
   [ !Bob_init( runid, $Bob, Kab ), In( Na ), In( senc(<Na, secret>, Kab) )
   ]
  --[
  Bob_2_0( runid, $Bob, Kab, Na, senc(<Na, secret>, Kab), <Na, secret> )
  ]->
   [ Bob_2_0( runid, $Bob, Kab, Na, senc(<Na, secret>, Kab), <Na, secret> )
   ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

rule (modulo E) Alice_1_2:
   [ !Alice_init( runid, $Alice, Kab, secret ), Fr( ~Na ) ]
  --[ Alice_1_2( runid, $Alice, Kab, secret, ~Na, senc(<Na, secret>, Kab) )
  ]->
   [
   Out( ~Na ), Out( senc(<Na, secret>, Kab) ),
   Alice_1_2( runid, $Alice, Kab, secret, ~Na, senc(<Na, secret>, Kab) )
   ]

  /*
  rule (modulo AC) Alice_1_2:
     [ !Alice_init( runid, $Alice, Kab, secret ), Fr( ~Na ) ]
    --[
    Alice_1_2( runid, $Alice, Kab, secret, ~Na, senc(<Na.1, secret>, Kab) )
    ]->
     [
     Out( ~Na ), Out( senc(<Na.1, secret>, Kab) ),
     Alice_1_2( runid, $Alice, Kab, secret, ~Na, senc(<Na.1, secret>, Kab) )
     ]
  */

rule (modulo E) privateReveal:
   [ !PrincipalPrivate( Principal, Private ) ]
  --[ Dishonest( Principal ) ]->
   [ Out( Private ) ]

  /* has exactly the trivial AC variant */

/*
WARNING: the following wellformedness checks failed!

unbound:
  rule `Alice_1_2' has unbound variables: 
    Na

sorts:
  rule `Alice_1_2' clashing sorts, casings, or multiplicities:
    1. ~Na, Na
*/

end
